# Marketing Analytics Master Topic Index
## Comprehensive Hierarchical Taxonomy for Marketing Analytics Professionals

---

**Version:** 12.0  
**Generated:** December 23, 2025  
**Last Updated:** December 26, 2025 (Batch 12 Final - All Sources Processed)  
**Sources:** Synthesized from 208+ source files in `topics/topic_inputs/` + ChatGPT & Claude conversation exports  

---

## Overview

This master index provides a comprehensive, 6-tier hierarchical taxonomy covering all aspects of the marketing analytics profession. The structure follows:

```
L1: Core Domain (12 pillars)
  L2: Major Category
    L3: Specialized Area
      L4: Technical Component
        L5: Specific Technique/Tool
          L6: Implementation Detail
```

---

# L1: FOUNDATIONS & CORE CONCEPTS

## L2: Analytics Frameworks & Methodologies

### L3: Analytics Types
- **L4: Descriptive Analytics** - Understanding what happened
  - L5: Historical Analysis
  - L5: Trend Identification
  - L5: Pattern Recognition
- **L4: Diagnostic Analytics** - Understanding why it happened
  - L5: Root Cause Analysis
  - L5: Variance Analysis
  - L5: Correlation Analysis
- **L4: Predictive Analytics** - Forecasting what will happen
  - L5: Statistical Forecasting
  - L5: Machine Learning Predictions
  - L5: Scenario Modeling
- **L4: Prescriptive Analytics** - Recommending what should happen
  - L5: Optimization Algorithms
  - L5: Decision Support Systems
  - L5: Automated Recommendations
- **L4: Real-Time Analytics** - Immediate insights and monitoring
  - L5: Streaming Data Analysis
  - L5: Live Dashboards
  - L5: Alerting Systems

### L3: Business Metrics Fundamentals
- **L4: KPI Design Principles**
  - L5: North Star Metric Selection
  - L5: KPI Trees / Metric Trees

  - L5: Metric Specification Sheets
- **L4: Metric Types**
  - L5: Leading vs Lagging Indicators
  - L5: Vanity Metrics vs Actionable Metrics
  - L5: Input vs Output Metrics
  - L5: Efficiency vs Effectiveness Metrics
- **L4: Goal Frameworks**
  - L5: S.M.A.R.T. Goals
  - L5: OKRs (Objectives & Key Results)
  - L5: AARRR (Pirate Metrics)
  - L5: HEART Framework

# L1: STATISTICAL METHODS & PROBABILITY

## L2: Probability & Distributions

### L3: Probability Theory
- **L4: Fundamental Concepts**
  - L5: Sample Space & Events
  - L5: Conditional Probability P(A|B) = P(A∩B) / P(B)
  - L5: Bayes' Theorem
  - L5: Independence
- **L4: Set Operations & Properties**
  - L5: Complement: P(A) + P(A') = 1
  - L5: Intersection: P(A∩B) = P(A)P(B) (for independent events)
  - L5: Union: P(A ∪ B) = P(A) + P(B) − P(A∩B)
  - L5: Independent Events (P(A|B) = P(A), P(B|A) = P(B))
  - L5: Mutually Exclusive Events: P(A∩B) = 0
- **L4: Common Distributions**
  - L5: Normal (Gaussian) Distribution
  - L5: Binomial Distribution
  - L5: Poisson Distribution
  - L5: Exponential Distribution
  - L5: Beta Distribution
- **L4: Central Limit Theorem**
  - L5: Sampling Distributions
  - L5: Standard Error
  - L5: Law of Large Numbers

### L3: Descriptive Statistics
- **L4: Measures of Central Tendency**
  - L5: Mean (Arithmetic, Geometric, Harmonic)
  - L5: Median
  - L5: Mode
  - L5: Trimmed Mean
- **L4: Measures of Variability**
  - L5: Range
  - L5: Variance
  - L5: Standard Deviation
  - L5: Coefficient of Variation
- **L4: Measures of Position**
  - L5: Percentiles
  - L5: Quartiles (Q1, Q2, Q3)
  - L5: Interquartile Range (IQR = Q3 - Q1)
  - L5: Z-Scores
- **L4: Distribution Shape**
  - L5: Skewness (Left/Right)
  - L5: Kurtosis (Leptokurtic, Platykurtic)
  - L5: Modality (Unimodal, Bimodal, Multimodal)

### L3: Product Experimentation Benefits
- **L4: Business Impact**
  - L5: Faster Decision-Making (Validated with Real User Data)
  - L5: Lower Risk (Test at Small Scale Before Full Rollout)
  - L5: Increased User Engagement (Data-Driven Optimization)
  - L5: Improved Product-Market Fit (Evidence-Based Features)
- **L4: When to Experiment**
  - L5: Validating New Feature Ideas
  - L5: Optimizing User Journeys
  - L5: Testing Pricing Changes
  - L5: Evaluating Personalization Strategies
- **L4: When NOT to Experiment**
  - L5: Legal/Compliance Requirements (Just Implement)
  - L5: Critical Bug Fixes (Deploy Immediately)
  - L5: Insufficient Traffic/Users (Use Qualitative Methods)
  - L5: Clear Directional Decisions (No Equipoise)

# L1: TEAM LEADERSHIP & CAREER DEVELOPMENT

## L2: Management Fundamentals

### L3: Core Management Concepts
- **L4: Four Functions of Management**
  - L5: Planning (Setting Objectives)
  - L5: Organizing (Arranging Resources)
  - L5: Leading (Motivating & Directing)
  - L5: Controlling (Monitoring & Correcting)
- **L4: Management Skills**
  - L5: Technical Skills (Analytics, SQL, Python)
  - L5: Human Skills (Communication, Empathy, Conflict Resolution)
  - L5: Conceptual Skills (Strategic Thinking, Systems Perspective)
- **L4: Leadership vs Management**
  - L5: Management (Processes, Stability, Execution)
  - L5: Leadership (Vision, Change, Inspiration)

### L3: Leadership Frameworks
- **L4: Situational Leadership (Blanchard & Hersey)**
  - L5: Directing (S1) - Low Competence, High Commitment
  - L5: Coaching (S2) - Some Competence, Low Commitment
  - L5: Supporting (S3) - High Competence, Variable Commitment
  - L5: Delegating (S4) - High Competence, High Commitment
- **L4: Tuckman's Team Development Stages**
  - L5: Forming (Unclear Roles)
  - L5: Storming (Conflicts Emerge)
  - L5: Norming (Cohesion Develops)
  - L5: Performing (High Productivity)
  - L5: Adjourning (Project Completion)
- **L4: DISC Assessment for Team Dynamics**
  - L5: Dominance (Results-Oriented, Direct)
  - L5: Influence (People-Oriented, Enthusiastic)
  - L5: Steadiness (Process-Oriented, Supportive)
  - L5: Conscientiousness (Detail-Oriented, Analytical)

### L3: Coaching & Development
- **L4: GROW Coaching Model**
  - L5: Goal (What to Achieve)
  - L5: Reality (Current Situation)
  - L5: Options (What Could You Do)
  - L5: Way Forward (What Will You Do)
- **L4: SBI Feedback Framework**
  - L5: Situation (When & Where)
  - L5: Behavior (What Was Done/Said)
  - L5: Impact (Effect on Others/Results)
- **L4: One-on-One Meeting Structure**
  - L5: Check-in (Personal Connection)
  - L5: Updates (Progress on Goals)
  - L5: Roadblocks (Challenges & Solutions)
  - L5: Growth (Career Development, Feedback)
  - L5: Action Items (Next Steps)

### L3: Prioritization Frameworks
- **L4: Eisenhower Matrix**
  - L5: Urgent + Important (Do First)
  - L5: Not Urgent + Important (Schedule)
  - L5: Urgent + Not Important (Delegate)
  - L5: Not Urgent + Not Important (Eliminate)
- **L4: RICE Scoring (Analytics Projects)**
  - L5: Reach (People/Decisions Affected)
  - L5: Impact (Value Created, 1-3 Scale)
  - L5: Confidence (Certainty Percentage)
  - L5: Effort (Person-Months Required)
- **L4: Analytics Project Prioritization**
  - L5: Business Impact (Revenue, Cost Savings)
  - L5: Technical Feasibility (Data Availability)
  - L5: Stakeholder Urgency (Executive Visibility)
  - L5: Team Development (Learning Opportunities)

### L3: Motivation Theories
- **L4: Maslow's Hierarchy (Applied to Work)**
  - L5: Physiological (Fair Compensation, Work-Life Balance)
  - L5: Safety (Job Security)
  - L5: Belonging (Team Culture, Inclusion)
  - L5: Esteem (Recognition, Achievement)
  - L5: Self-Actualization (Growth, Meaningful Work)
- **L4: Herzberg's Two-Factor Theory**
  - L5: Hygiene Factors (Salary, Conditions, Policies)
  - L5: Motivators (Achievement, Recognition, Growth, Responsibility)
- **L4: Daniel Pink's Drive Framework**
  - L5: Autonomy (Control Over Work)
  - L5: Mastery (Getting Better at Something Important)
  - L5: Purpose (Contributing to Something Larger)

# APPENDIX: QUICK REFERENCE

## Common Terms & Vocabulary

### Experimentation Terms
- **Counterfactual** - What would have happened without the intervention
- **MDE (Minimum Detectable Effect)** - Smallest effect the experiment can reliably detect
- **SRM (Sample Ratio Mismatch)** - Deviation from expected treatment/control split
- **CUPED** - Controlled-experiment Using Pre-Experiment Data
- **Power** - Probability of detecting a true effect

### Attribution Terms
- **iROAS** - Incremental Return on Ad Spend
- **Marginal ROAS** - Return on the next dollar spent
- **Adstock** - Carryover effect of advertising over time
- **Saturation** - Diminishing returns at high spend levels

### Measurement Terms
- **Incrementality** - True causal impact (vs. correlated behavior)
- **Cannibalization** - New channel stealing credit from existing channels
- **Halo Effect** - Positive spillover to related products/channels
- **Calibration** - Adjusting models using experimental results

### Statistical Terms
- **Type I Error (α)** - False positive, rejecting a true null hypothesis
- **Type II Error (β)** - False negative, failing to reject a false null
- **Confidence Interval** - Range likely to contain true parameter value
- **P-value** - Probability of results if null hypothesis is true
- **Effect Size** - Magnitude of difference between groups

### Platform & Technical Terms
- **Feature Flag** - Toggle to enable/disable features for user segments
- **Bucketing** - Assigning users to experiment variants
- **Exposure Logging** - Recording when users see experimental changes
- **Trigger** - Event that qualifies a user for experiment inclusion
- **SUTVA** - Stable Unit Treatment Value Assumption (no interference)

---

## Quick-Start Checklists

### Design Phase Checklist
- [ ] Clear hypothesis with testable prediction
- [ ] Primary metric (OEC) and guardrail metrics defined
- [ ] Sample size calculated with power ≥ 80%
- [ ] MDE aligned with business significance
- [ ] Randomization unit selected (user/session/geo)
- [ ] Eligibility criteria defined
- [ ] Success criteria and decision rules documented
- [ ] Pre-registration completed

### Implementation Checklist
- [ ] Feature flag configured correctly
- [ ] Event tracking implemented and verified
- [ ] Exposure logging working
- [ ] A/A test passed (no false positives)
- [ ] Canary deployment successful
- [ ] Monitoring dashboards set up
- [ ] Kill-switch tested

### Analysis Phase Checklist
- [ ] SRM check passed
- [ ] Data quality validated
- [ ] Primary metric analyzed with CI
- [ ] Guardrail metrics reviewed
- [ ] Segment analysis completed (if pre-registered)
- [ ] Novelty effect assessed
- [ ] External validity considered

### Decision & Rollout Checklist
- [ ] Results meet statistical significance threshold
- [ ] Results meet practical significance threshold
- [ ] Stakeholder alignment achieved
- [ ] Rollout plan documented
- [ ] Holdout group maintained (if applicable)
- [ ] Learnings documented in repository
- [ ] Knowledge shared with team

---

## Learning Path Recommendations

### Foundational Track (0-6 months)
1. Statistics fundamentals & hypothesis testing
2. SQL basics & data manipulation
3. Web analytics & digital marketing metrics
4. Basic visualization & reporting

### Intermediate Track (6-12 months)
1. Customer segmentation & CLV modeling
2. Attribution modeling concepts
3. A/B testing & experimentation
4. Marketing mix modeling basics
5. Python/R programming

### Advanced Track (12+ months)
1. Machine learning for marketing
2. Advanced experimentation (causal inference)
3. Advanced MMM & incrementality
4. Marketing automation & optimization
5. MLOps & model deployment

# L1: INTERVIEW PREPARATION & PROBLEM SOLVING

## L2: Probability Interview Problems

### L3: Easy Difficulty (FAANG & Tech)
- **L4: Conditional Probability (Facebook, Amazon)**
  - L5: Coin Fairness Test (Unfair vs Fair Coin)
  - L5: Disease Testing (Base Rate Fallacy)
  - L5: Bayes' Theorem Applications
  - L5: Diligent vs Non-Diligent Rater Problem
- **L4: Basic Probability (Tesla, Google)**
  - L5: Die Rolling Probabilities
  - L5: Card Drawing Problems (Color, Number Matching)
  - L5: Seven-Game Series Probability
- **L4: Expected Value (Microsoft, Facebook)**
  - L5: Expected Rolls to See All Faces
  - L5: Coupon Collector Problem
  - L5: Expected Time to Completion
- **L4: Sequential Probability (Lyft, Uber)**
  - L5: Coin Flipping Games (HH vs TH)
  - L5: Probability of Winning Sequences
  - L5: Strictly Increasing Order

### L3: Medium Difficulty (Tech & Finance)
- **L4: Geometric Problems (Bloomberg)**
  - L5: Chord Intersection Probability
  - L5: Ant Walking Problems (Triangle Corners)
  - L5: Polygon Collision Avoidance
- **L4: Sequential Events (Two Sigma, Amazon)**
  - L5: Expected Flips for Consecutive Heads
  - L5: Expected Cards to First Ace
  - L5: First Success Problems
- **L4: Game Theory (Robinhood, Airbnb)**
  - L5: Coin Comparison Games (n+1 vs n coins)
  - L5: Fair Odds from Unfair Coins
  - L5: Generating Fair Outcomes
- **L4: Distribution Problems (Quora, Spotify)**
  - L5: Normal Distribution Exceedance
  - L5: Probability k > Y for N draws
  - L5: Maximum of n Dice Rolls

### L3: Hard Difficulty (Hedge Funds & Advanced Tech)
- **L4: Complex Combinatorics (Snapchat)**
  - L5: Mutual Best Friends Probability
  - L5: Matching Problems
  - L5: Random Permutation Properties
- **L4: Stochastic Processes (Tesla)**
  - L5: Vehicle Replacement Frequency
  - L5: Long-term Equilibrium
  - L5: Renewal Theory Applications
- **L4: Advanced Sampling (Spotify)**
  - L5: Maximum Order Statistics
  - L5: Distribution of Max in n Rolls
  - L5: Extreme Value Theory

## L2: Statistics Interview Problems

### L3: Conceptual Questions (Easy)
- **L4: Statistical Concepts (Facebook, Microsoft)**
  - L5: Explaining Confidence Intervals to Non-Technical Audiences
  - L5: P-values in Layman's Terms
  - L5: Power & Sample Size Intuition
- **L4: A/B Testing Fundamentals (Twitter, Uber)**
  - L5: Common A/B Testing Pitfalls
  - L5: When to Stop a Test
  - L5: Multiple Comparisons Problem

### L3: Technical Problems (Medium)
- **L4: Estimation Problems (Stripe, Google)**
  - L5: Exponential Distribution Parameter Estimation
  - L5: Uniform Distribution Max Estimation
  - L5: Expected Value Derivations (Geometric, Uniform)
- **L4: Hypothesis Testing (Lyft, Robinhood)**
  - L5: Coin Bias Detection (1000 flips, 550 heads)
  - L5: Deriving CIs from Coin Tosses
  - L5: Permutation Swap Expected Value
- **L4: Metric Comparison (Facebook, Google)**
  - L5: Comparing Ranked Lists (Movie Preferences)
  - L5: Blending Means & SDs from Subsets
  - L5: Extending to K Subsets

### L3: Advanced Statistical Theory (Hard)
- **L4: MLE vs MAP (Uber, Two Sigma)**
  - L5: Mathematical Derivation
  - L5: Practical Differences
  - L5: Prior Selection Impact
- **L4: Distribution Sampling (Lyft, Two Sigma)**
  - L5: Uniform Sampling from Circle
  - L5: Expected Samples Until Sum Exceeds 1
  - L5: Generating Normal from Bernoulli
- **L4: Regression Challenges (Two Sigma)**
  - L5: Multicollinearity Detection & Solutions
  - L5: Correlated Predictors Impact
  - L5: Regularization for Correlated Features

# L1: EXPERIMENTATION & A/B TESTING (COMPREHENSIVE)

## L2: Pre-Experiment Planning

### L3: Business Objective Definition
- **L4: Goal Types**
  - L5: Revenue Optimization
  - L5: Conversion Rate Improvement
  - L5: Customer Acquisition Cost Reduction
  - L5: Lifetime Value Increase
  - L5: Engagement Metrics Improvement
  - L5: Retention Improvement
- **L4: Success Metrics**
  - L5: Primary Metrics (North Star)
  - L5: Secondary Metrics
  - L5: Guardrail Metrics
  - L5: Counter Metrics
  - L5: Leading vs Lagging Indicators

### L3: Hypothesis Frameworks
- **L4: Hypothesis Formats**
  - L5: If-Then-Because Format
  - L5: Problem-Solution-Result
  - L5: Jobs-to-be-Done Hypothesis
  - L5: Lean Hypothesis
  - L5: Scientific Method

## L2: Experiment Type Selection

### L3: Basic Experiment Types
- **L4: A/B Testing**
  - L5: Single Variable Change
  - L5: Clear Binary Choices
  - L5: Statistical Significance Testing
- **L4: A/B/n Testing**
  - L5: Multiple Variants
  - L5: Optimization Curve Exploration
- **L4: Multivariate Testing (MVT)**
  - L5: Multiple Variables Simultaneously
  - L5: Interaction Effects Analysis

### L3: Advanced Experiment Types
- **L4: Multi-Armed Bandit (MAB)**
  - L5: Dynamic Allocation
  - L5: Epsilon-Greedy Algorithm
  - L5: Thompson Sampling
  - L5: Upper Confidence Bound (UCB)
- **L4: Factorial Design**
  - L5: Full Factorial (All Combinations)
  - L5: Fractional Factorial
- **L4: Sequential Testing**
  - L5: Early Stopping Rules
  - L5: Adaptive Designs
- **L4: Switchback Testing**
  - L5: Time-Based Allocation
  - L5: Network Effects Handling
- **L4: Synthetic Control**
  - L5: No Randomization Possible
  - L5: Market-Level Rollouts
  - L5: Causal Inference

## L2: Statistical Framework

### L3: Statistical Test Selection
- **L4: Parametric Tests**
  - L5: Z-Test (Large Samples, Known Variance)
  - L5: Student's T-Test (Small Samples)
  - L5: Welch's T-Test (Unequal Variances)
  - L5: ANOVA (Multiple Groups)
- **L4: Non-Parametric Tests**
  - L5: Mann-Whitney U Test
  - L5: Kolmogorov-Smirnov Test
  - L5: Chi-Square Test (Categorical Data)
  - L5: Fisher's Exact Test (Small Samples)
- **L4: Advanced Methods**
  - L5: Bootstrap Methods
  - L5: Bayesian Methods
  - L5: CUPED/CUPAC (Variance Reduction)

### L3: Power Analysis & Sample Size
- **L4: Key Parameters**
  - L5: Statistical Power (1-β, Typically 0.8)
  - L5: Significance Level (α, Typically 0.05)
  - L5: Minimum Detectable Effect (MDE)
  - L5: Baseline Conversion Rate
- **L4: Sample Size Methods**
  - L5: Classical Power Analysis
  - L5: Sequential Analysis
  - L5: Bayesian Sample Size
  - L5: Simulation-Based (Monte Carlo)

## L2: Randomization & Implementation

### L3: Randomization Strategies
- **L4: Randomization Methods**
  - L5: Simple Random Assignment
  - L5: Block Randomization
  - L5: Stratified Randomization
  - L5: Cluster Randomization
  - L5: Matched Pairs
- **L4: Technical Implementation**
  - L5: Hash-Based (Deterministic)
  - L5: Time-Based Allocation
  - L5: Geo-Based Randomization

### L3: Implementation Frameworks
- **L4: Testing Platforms**
  - L5: Feature Flags (LaunchDarkly, Split.io)
  - L5: Commercial (Optimizely, Adobe Target, VWO)
  - L5: Analytics-Integrated (Amplitude Experiment, Statsig)
  - L5: Open Source (GrowthBook, Wasabi)
- **L4: Implementation Types**
  - L5: Server-Side Testing
  - L5: Client-Side Testing
  - L5: Edge Computing
  - L5: Mobile SDKs

  - L5: Covariate Balance Check

  - L5: Canary Deployment (1% → 5% → 25% → 50%)

  - L5: Bayes Factors

### L3: Advanced Techniques

  - L5: CUPED (Pre-Experiment Data)
  - L5: Stratified Estimators
- **L4: Causal Inference**
  - L5: Difference-in-Differences (DiD)
  - L5: Regression Discontinuity
  - L5: Instrumental Variables
  - L5: Propensity Score Matching
- **L4: Heterogeneous Effects**
  - L5: Subgroup Analysis
  - L5: Interaction Terms
  - L5: Causal Forests

### L3: Interpretation Framework
- **L4: Statistical Interpretation**
  - L5: Practical vs Statistical Significance
  - L5: Effect Size Reporting
  - L5: Multiple Testing Correction
- **L4: Decision Frameworks**
  - L5: Hypothesis Testing (p < α)
  - L5: Bayesian Decision (P(lift>0) > 0.95)
  - L5: Risk-Adjusted (Worst-Case Scenario)
  - L5: Portfolio Approach

## L2: Post-Experiment Actions

### L3: Implementation Strategies
- **L4: Rollout Approaches**
  - L5: Full Rollout (100% Immediate)
  - L5: Gradual Rollout (50% → 75% → 100%)
  - L5: Holdout Groups (5-10% Control)
  - L5: Segment-Based Rollout
- **L4: Feature Flag Management**
  - L5: Instant Rollback Capability
  - L5: Progressive Delivery

### L3: Knowledge Management
- **L4: Documentation**
  - L5: Experiment Briefs
  - L5: Analysis Notebooks
  - L5: Decision Logs
- **L4: Organizational Learning**
  - L5: Cross-Experiment Analysis
  - L5: Pattern Recognition
  - L5: Failure Analysis
  - L5: Meta-Learning

## L2: Experimentation Maturity Framework

### L3: Level 1: Ad-Hoc Testing
- **L4: Characteristics**
  - L5: Individual Contributor Level
  - L5: Basic A/B Tests
  - L5: Manual Analysis
  - L5: No Formal Process

### L3: Level 2: Systematic Testing
- **L4: Characteristics**
  - L5: Structured Processes
  - L5: Dedicated Testing Team
  - L5: Standardized Metrics
  - L5: Basic Power Analysis

### L3: Level 3: Advanced Experimentation
- **L4: Characteristics**
  - L5: Embedded Data Scientists
  - L5: Sophisticated Methods (CUPED, Bayesian)
  - L5: Experimentation Platform
  - L5: Cross-Functional Integration

- **L4: Characteristics**
  - L5: Organization-Wide Capability
  - L5: Strategic Integration
  - L5: Autonomous Optimization
  - L5: AI-Augmented Testing

# L1: FINANCIAL & REVENUE ANALYTICS

## L2: Core Financial Metrics

### L3: Acquisition Metrics

  - L5: CAC = Total Acquisition Spend / New Customers
  - L5: CAC by Channel
  - L5: Blended vs Paid CAC

  - L5: Healthy Ratio (3:1 or higher)
  - L5: Payback Period

### L3: Efficiency Metrics
- **L4: Return on Ad Spend (ROAS)**
  - L5: ROAS = Revenue / Ad Spend
  - L5: iROAS (Incremental ROAS)
- **L4: Marketing Efficiency Ratio (MER)**
  - L5: MER = Total Revenue / Total Marketing Spend
- **L4: Return on Investment (ROI)**
  - L5: ROI = (Revenue - Cost) / Cost

# L1: ANALYTICS TRANSFORMATION ROADMAP

## L2: Year 1 - Infrastructure, Trust & Descriptive Analytics

### L3: Phase 1 - Audit, Architecture & Hygiene (Months 1-3)
- **L4: Tracking Audit (Client-Side)**
  - L5: Tag Management System (TMS) Governance
  - L5: Container Structure & Ghost Tag Cleanup
  - L5: Trigger Logic Improvement (URL-based to customEvent)
  - L5: Data Layer Object (DLO) Schema Definition
- **L4: Cookie Consent & Legal Compliance**
  - L5: CMP Integration (OneTrust/Cookiebot)
  - L5: PII Redaction & Regex Filters
- **L4: Cross-Domain & App Tracking**
  - L5: Measurement Protocol Configuration
  - L5: Firebase/Mobile SDK Unification
- **L4: Modern Data Stack (MDS) Implementation**
  - L5: ELT Pipeline Selection (Fivetran, Airbyte)
  - L5: Connector Configuration (Ad Platforms, Transactional, Email/SMS)
  - L5: Schema Architecture (Bronze/Silver/Gold Layers)
- **L4: Taxonomy & Standardization**
  - L5: UTM Consensus & Enforcement
  - L5: Campaign Naming Convention (Region_Channel_Objective_Date_CreativeID)

### L3: Phase 2 - Business Logic, Reporting & Financial Alignment (Months 4-6)
- **L4: Financial Reconciliation**
  - L5: Definition of "Revenue" (GA4 vs ERP)
  - L5: Variance Analysis (<5% drift)
  - L5: Return/Refund Logic
- **L4: Cost Calculation**
  - L5: "All-in" Loading (Agency Fees, Tool Costs, Creative Production)
  - L5: True ROAS vs Media ROAS
- **L4: Visualization & Dashboard Engineering**
  - L5: Cognitive Load Management
  - L5: Preattentive Attributes (Color for Good/Bad only)
- **L4: Three-Tiered Dashboard Suite**
  - L5: Tier 1: Board Deck (Strategic) - Monthly
  - L5: Tier 2: Marketing Pulse (Operational) - Daily
  - L5: Tier 3: Exploratory Workbench (Tactical)
- **L4: Baseline Statistical Profiling**
  - L5: Control Charting (Rolling Means, ±2σ Thresholds)
  - L5: Automated Alerts (Slack/Email)

### L3: Phase 3 - Resilience, Retention & Advanced Segmentation (Months 7-9)
- **L4: Signal Resilience (Fighting ITP & Cookie Loss)**
  - L5: Server-Side Tracking (CAPI) Implementation
  - L5: Meta Conversions API & Google Enhanced Conversions
  - L5: De-duplication Keys (event_id matching)
- **L4: First-Party Data Enrichment**
  - L5: Lead Scoring Models (Explicit + Implicit)
  - L5: Zero-Party Data Capture (Post-purchase surveys)
- **L4: Advanced Segmentation (Clustering)**
  - L5: RFM Analysis (Recency, Frequency, Monetary)
  - L5: K-Means Clustering (Python/Scikit-Learn)
  - L5: Elbow Method for Optimal k
- **L4: Retention Mechanics**
  - L5: Cohort Analysis (Triangle Charts)
  - L5: Churn Definitions (Logo Churn, Net Revenue Churn)

### L3: Phase 4 - Testing & Optimization Strategy (Months 10-12)
- **L4: Experimentation Framework (CRO)**
  - L5: Power Analysis (Pre-test Sample Size)
  - L5: Significance Thresholds (α = 0.05 vs α = 0.10)
  - L5: SRM Checks (Sample Ratio Mismatch)
- **L4: Test Hierarchy**
  - L5: Macro Tests (Value Proposition, Pricing)
  - L5: Micro Tests (Button color, CTA text)
- **L4: Efficiency & Pacing**
  - L5: Budget Pacing Algorithms & Burn Rate
  - L5: Marginal ROAS Analysis & Diminishing Returns

## L2: Year 2 - Predictive Analytics, Causality & AI

  - L5: Bayes' Theorem Application

  - L5: 95% CI Interpretation

  - L5: Formula: (X - μ) / σ

  - L5: Poisson vs Binomial (Fixed interval vs Fixed trials)
- **L4: Error Types**
  - L5: Type I Error (Reject true null)
  - L5: Type II Error (Fail to reject false null)
- **L4: Maximum Likelihood Estimation (MLE)**
  - L5: Parameter Estimation via Likelihood Maximization
- **L4: Covariance vs Correlation**
  - L5: Covariance: Degree of joint change
  - L5: Correlation: Strength & direction of linear relationship
- **L4: Stratified Sampling**
  - L5: Advantages over Simple Random Sampling

# L1: PRODUCT METRICS CASE STUDIES (Airbnb-Style)

## L2: Structured Analytical Approach Framework

### L3: Step 1 - Clarify the Problem
- **L4: Understanding Elements**
  - L5: Business Objective
  - L5: Scope (Geography, Time Period, User Segment)
  - L5: Stakeholders and Goals

### L3: Step 2 - Define Success Metrics
- **L4: Metric Categories**
  - L5: Primary Metric (Main KPI)
  - L5: Secondary Metrics (Supporting Indicators)
  - L5: Guardrail Metrics (Things to Protect)
  - L5: Counter Metrics (Potential Negative Side Effects)

### L3: Step 3 - Structure Your Analysis
- **L4: Analysis Components**
  - L5: Break Down Metric into Components (Funnels, Formulas)
  - L5: Identify Issue/Opportunity Location
  - L5: Form Hypotheses about Root Causes

### L3: Step 4 - Recommend Approach
- **L4: Recommendation Elements**
  - L5: Data Requirements
  - L5: Analysis Plan
  - L5: Validation Methods

## L2: Case Study Templates

### L3: Case Study 1 - Booking Conversion Drop
- **L4: Clarify**
  - L5: Time Period (vs What Baseline?)
  - L5: Geography (Global or Specific Markets?)
  - L5: Platform (Web, iOS, Android?)
  - L5: User Segment (New vs Returning?)
- **L4: Metrics**
  - L5: Primary: Booking Conversion Rate = Bookings / Searches
  - L5: Secondary: Search-to-inquiry rate, Inquiry-to-booking rate
  - L5: Guardrail: Revenue per booking, Guest satisfaction
  - L5: Counter: Host acceptance rate
- **L4: Funnel Breakdown**
  - L5: Search → View Listings → Click Listing → View Details → Inquire → Book
- **L4: Hypothesis Areas**
  - L5: Supply (Availability, Pricing, Quality)
  - L5: Demand (Seasonal, Marketing Mix, Intent)
  - L5: Product (Feature Changes, A/B Tests, Algorithm)
  - L5: Technical (Page Load, Bugs, Payment Issues)
  - L5: External (Competitors, Economic, Restrictions)
- **L4: Analysis Approach**
  - L5: Segmentation Analysis (Device, Geography, User Type)
  - L5: Cohort Analysis
  - L5: Funnel Analysis
  - L5: Time Series Analysis
  - L5: A/B Test Review

### L3: Case Study 2 - New Feature Impact
- **L4: Clarify**
  - L5: Who Sees Feature? (All Users or Segments?)
  - L5: Where in Booking Flow?
  - L5: Business Goal (Bookings? Occupancy? Satisfaction?)
- **L4: Metrics for "Flexible Dates" Feature**
  - L5: Primary: Booking conversion, Bookings per user, GBV
  - L5: Secondary: Feature engagement, Search-to-booking time
  - L5: Guardrail: Revenue per booking, Host earnings, NPS
  - L5: Counter: Original date abandonment, Lower ADR
- **L4: Experiment Design**
  - L5: Test Setup (Control vs Treatment)
  - L5: Sample Size Calculation
  - L5: Duration (2-4 weeks for seasonality)
  - L5: Randomization (User-level)
- **L4: Analysis Plan**
  - L5: Week 1: Technical Issues, SRM Monitoring
  - L5: During: Daily Metrics, Engagement Tracking
  - L5: Post: Statistical Significance, HTE Analysis
- **L4: Decision Framework**
  - L5: Ship if: ↑ Bookings AND No Negative Revenue/Host Impact
  - L5: Iterate if: High Engagement, Mixed Booking Results
  - L5: Kill if: No Engagement OR Negative Key Metrics

### L3: Case Study 3 - Two-Sided Marketplace Imbalance
- **L4: Problem Definition**
  - L5: Supply-Demand Imbalance (Host ↑30% vs Guest ↑10%)
- **L4: Potential Issues**
  - L5: Lower Host Occupancy → Frustration → Churn
  - L5: Pricing Pressure (More Supply = Lower Prices)
  - L5: Quality Dilution
  - L5: Search Experience Degradation
- **L4: Key Metrics**
  - L5: Host Side: Occupancy Rate, Earnings, Time to First Booking, Retention
  - L5: Guest Side: Search Results, Conversion, Satisfaction
  - L5: Marketplace: Supply Utilization, Take Rate, Concentration
- **L4: Analysis Dimensions**
  - L5: Geographic Analysis (Market-level Imbalance)
  - L5: Host Quality (New Host Quality Distribution)
  - L5: Guest Demand (Search Volume, Find What Looking For?)
  - L5: Segment Analysis (Property Types vs Search Patterns)
- **L4: Recommendations**
  - L5: Short-term: Pause Host Acquisition in Oversupplied Markets
  - L5: Medium-term: Focus Guest Acquisition, Host Quality Scoring
  - L5: Long-term: Predictive Models, Market-specific Strategies

## L2: Key Interview Tips

### L3: Communication Best Practices
- **L4: Approach**
  - L5: Always Start with Clarifying Questions
  - L5: Think Out Loud
  - L5: Use Frameworks (Funnels, Formulas, Segmentation)
  - L5: Consider Trade-offs
  - L5: Be Hypothesis-Driven ("I would check if...")
  - L5: Think Two-Sided Marketplace (Hosts AND Guests)
  - L5: Mention Data Validation (Seasonality, External Factors)
  - L5: Connect to Business Impact (Revenue, not just "metric went up")

  - L5: Retriever, Generator, Knowledge Base

# L1: MARKETING EXPERIMENTATION FRAMEWORK (Comprehensive)

## L2: Experiment Type Selection

### L3: Test Types
- **L4: A/B Testing**
  - L5: Single Variable Change, Binary Choices
- **L4: A/B/n Testing**
  - L5: Multiple Variants, Optimization Curve
- **L4: Multivariate Testing (MVT)**
  - L5: Multiple Variables, Interaction Effects
- **L4: Multi-Armed Bandit**
  - L5: Dynamic Allocation, Continuous Optimization
- **L4: Factorial Design**
  - L5: Full Factorial, Fractional Factorial
- **L4: Sequential Testing**
  - L5: Early Stopping Rules, Adaptive Designs
- **L4: Switchback Testing**
  - L5: Time-Based Allocation, Network Effects
- **L4: Synthetic Control**
  - L5: No Randomization Possible, Causal Inference

## L2: Statistical Framework

### L3: Statistical Test Selection
- **L4: Parametric Tests**
  - L5: Z-Test (Large Samples)
  - L5: T-Test (Small Samples)
  - L5: Welch's T-Test (Unequal Variances)
- **L4: Non-Parametric Tests**
  - L5: Mann-Whitney U
  - L5: Chi-Square, Fisher's Exact
- **L4: Advanced Methods**
  - L5: Bayesian Methods
  - L5: CUPED/CUPAC Variance Reduction
  - L5: Bootstrap Methods

### L3: Sample Size Calculation
- **L4: Methods**
  - L5: Classical Power Analysis
  - L5: Minimum Detectable Effect (MDE)
  - L5: Sequential Analysis
  - L5: Simulation-Based

## L2: Experiment Design & Implementation

### L3: Randomization Strategies
- **L4: Types**
  - L5: Simple Random, Block, Stratified
  - L5: Cluster, Matched Pairs
  - L5: Hash-Based, Time-Based, Geo-Based

### L3: Implementation Frameworks
- **L4: Feature Flags**
  - L5: LaunchDarkly, Optimizely, Split.io
- **L4: Server-Side Testing**
  - L5: Backend Randomization, API-Driven
- **L4: Client-Side Testing**
  - L5: JavaScript-Based, Google Optimize
- **L4: Full-Stack Platforms**
  - L5: Amplitude Experiment, Statsig, Eppo

## L2: Monitoring & Quality Assurance

- **L4: Validation**
  - L5: AA Testing
  - L5: Sample Ratio Mismatch (SRM)
  - L5: Covariate Balance
  - L5: Technical Validation

### L3: Runtime Monitoring
- **L4: Metrics**
  - L5: Statistical Significance Tracking
  - L5: Practical Significance
  - L5: Data Quality, System Health

  - L5: Hypothesis Testing, Confidence Intervals

  - L5: Posterior Distributions, Credible Intervals

  - L5: ANCOVA, Propensity Scores
- **L4: Machine Learning**
  - L5: Causal Forests, Double ML

### L3: Advanced Techniques
- **L4: Variance Reduction**
  - L5: CUPED (Pre-experiment Data)

  - L5: Difference-in-Differences
  - L5: Instrumental Variables
  - L5: Regression Discontinuity
- **L4: Heterogeneous Effects**
  - L5: Subgroup Analysis
  - L5: Quantile Treatment Effects

  - L5: Novelty Effects, Seasonality

  - L5: Hypothesis Testing (p < α)
  - L5: Bayesian Decision (Expected Utility)
  - L5: Risk-Adjusted Decisions

  - L5: Full Rollout, Gradual Rollout
  - L5: Holdout Groups, Regional Rollout

  - L5: Experiment Briefs, Analysis Notebooks
  - L5: Decision Logs

  - L5: Cross-Experiment Analysis

  - L5: Page Layout, Form Fields

  - L5: Subject Lines, Personalization

  - L5: Badges, Privacy Seals

## L2: Common Pitfalls & Solutions

### L3: Issues
- **L4: Peeking (Early Stopping)**
  - L5: Use Fixed Sample or Bayesian Stopping
- **L4: High Metric Variance**
  - L5: Log Transformation, Median
- **L4: Winner's Curse**
  - L5: Re-test Before Full Rollout
- **L4: Low Power**
  - L5: Increase Duration/Sample Size
- **L4: Overlapping Experiments**
  - L5: Mutual Exclusivity Buckets

## Document Summary

This master topic index now represents **Version 11.0** with content synthesized from **205+ source files**, providing a comprehensive 6-tier hierarchical taxonomy covering:

1. **Core Marketing Analytics Foundations** - Metrics, measurement, statistical methods
2. **Customer Analytics** - Segmentation, CLV, journey analytics, behavioral analysis
3. **Marketing Performance** - Attribution, MMM, incrementality testing
4. **Channel Analytics** - Digital, social, email, content, paid media
5. **Advanced Analytics** - ML/AI, real-time analytics, predictive modeling
6. **Experimentation** - A/B testing, statistical methods, trustworthy experiments
7. **Data Infrastructure** - Governance, quality, privacy, compliance
8. **Organizational & Career** - Team structures, role competencies, career paths
9. **Industry Applications** - E-commerce, B2B, fintech, retail
10. **Emerging Trends** - AI/GenAI, privacy evolution, edge analytics

**Total L1 Sections:** 40+
**Total L2 Categories:** 200+
**Total Topics (L3-L6):** 3,500+
